# <a name="routing-in-aspnet-core"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-103">ASP.NET Core에서 라우팅</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-103">Routing in ASP.NET Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-104">작성자: [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5) 및 [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-104">By [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5), and [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span></span>

::: moniker range=">= aspnetcore-3.0"

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-105">라우팅은 들어오는 HTTP 요청을 일치시켜 앱의 실행 가능 엔드포인트로 디스패치하는 역할을 담당합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-105">Routing is responsible for matching incoming HTTP requests and dispatching those requests to the app's executable endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-106">[엔드포인트](#endpoint)는 앱의 실행 가능 요청 처리 코드 단위입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-106">[Endpoints](#endpoint) are the app's units of executable request-handling code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-107">엔드포인트는 앱에서 정의되고 앱 시작 시 구성됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-107">Endpoints are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-108">엔드포인트 일치 프로세스는 요청의 URL에서 값을 추출하고 요청 처리를 위해 이 값을 제공할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-108">The endpoint matching process can extract values from the request's URL and provide those values for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-109">또한 라우팅은 앱의 엔드포인트 정보를 사용하여 엔드포인트에 매핑되는 URL을 생성할 수도 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-109">Using endpoint information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-110">앱은 다음을 사용하여 라우팅을 구성할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-110">Apps can configure routing using:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="d8913-111">Controllers</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-111">Controllers</span></span>
- Razor<span data-ttu-id="d8913-112"> Pages</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-112"> Pages</span></span>
- SignalR
- <span data-ttu-id="d8913-113">gRPC 서비스</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-113">gRPC Services</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="d8913-114">[상태 검사](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks)와 같은 엔드포인트 지원 [미들웨어](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-114">Endpoint-enabled [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) such as [Health Checks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="d8913-115">라우팅에 등록된 대리자 및 람다</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-115">Delegates and lambdas registered with routing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-116">이 문서에서는 ASP.NET Core 라우팅의 하위 수준 세부 정보를 설명합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-116">This document covers low-level details of ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-117">라우팅을 구성하는 방법은 다음을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-117">For information on configuring routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-118">컨트롤러의 경우 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-118">For controllers, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-119">Razor Pages 규칙은 <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-119">For Razor Pages conventions, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-120">이 문서에서 설명하는 엔드포인트 라우팅 시스템은 ASP.NET Core 3.0 이상에 적용됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-120">The endpoint routing system described in this document applies to ASP.NET Core 3.0 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-121"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 기반의 이전 라우팅 시스템에 대한 자세한 내용은 다음 접근 방법 중 하나를 사용하여 ASP.NET Core 2.1 버전을 선택합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-121">For information on the previous routing system based on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, select the ASP.NET Core 2.1 version using one of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-122">이전 버전의 버전 선택기</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-122">The version selector for a previous version.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-123">[ASP.NET Core 2.1 라우팅](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1) 선택</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-123">Select [ASP.NET Core 2.1 routing](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-124">[예제 코드 살펴보기 및 다운로드](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([다운로드 방법](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-124">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-125">이 문서의 다운로드 샘플은 특정 `Startup` 클래스를 통해 사용할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-125">The download samples for this document are enabled by a specific `Startup` class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-126">특정 샘플을 실행하려면 *Program.cs*를 수정하여 원하는 `Startup` 클래스를 호출합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-126">To run a specific sample, modify *Program.cs* to call the desired `Startup` class.</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-127">라우팅 기본 사항</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-127">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-128">모든 ASP.NET Core 템플릿에는 생성된 코드에서의 라우팅이 포함됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-128">All ASP.NET Core templates include routing in the generated code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-129">라우팅은 `Startup.Configure`의 [미들웨어](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) 파이프라인에 등록됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-129">Routing is registered in the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline in `Startup.Configure`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-130">다음 코드에서는 라우팅의 기본 예제를 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-130">The following code shows a basic example of routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet&highlight=8,10)]

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-131">라우팅은 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> 및 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>를 통해 등록된 미들웨어 쌍을 사용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-131">Routing uses a pair of middleware, registered by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-132">`UseRouting`은 경로 일치를 미들웨어 파이프라인에 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-132">`UseRouting` adds route matching to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-133">이 미들웨어는 앱에 정의된 엔드포인트 집합을 확인하고 요청을 기반으로 [가장 일치하는 항목](#urlm)을 선택합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-133">This middleware looks at the set of endpoints defined in the app, and selects the [best match](#urlm) based on the request.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-134">`UseEndpoints`는 엔드포인트 실행을 미들웨어 파이프라인에 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-134">`UseEndpoints` adds endpoint execution to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-135">선택한 엔드포인트와 연결된 대리자를 실행합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-135">It runs the delegate associated with the selected endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-136">앞의 예제에는 [MapGet](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*) 메서드를 사용하는 단일 ‘라우팅 대상 코드’ 엔드포인트가 포함됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-136">The preceding example includes a single *route to code* endpoint using the [MapGet](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*) method:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-137">HTTP `GET` 요청이 루트 URL `/`로 전송되면 다음과 같이 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-137">When an HTTP `GET` request is sent to the root URL `/`:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-138">표시된 요청 대리자가 실행됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-138">The request delegate shown executes.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-139">`Hello World!`가 HTTP 응답에 기록됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-139">`Hello World!` is written to the HTTP response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-140">기본적으로 루트 URL `/`는 `https://localhost:5001/`입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-140">By default, the root URL `/` is `https://localhost:5001/`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-141">요청 메서드가 `GET`이 아니거나 루트 URL이 `/`가 아니면 일치하는 경로가 없고 HTTP 404가 반환됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-141">If the request method is not `GET` or the root URL is not `/`, no route matches and an HTTP 404 is returned.</span></span>

### <a name="endpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-142">엔드포인트</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-142">Endpoint</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-143">`MapGet` 메서드는 **엔드포인트**을 정의하는 데 사용됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-143">The `MapGet` method is used to define an **endpoint**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-144">엔드포인트는 다음과 같을 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-144">An endpoint is something that can be:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-145">URL 및 HTTP 메서드를 일치시켜 선택됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-145">Selected, by matching the URL and HTTP method.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-146">대리자를 실행하여 실행됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-146">Executed, by running the delegate.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-147">앱에서 일치시키고 실행할 수 있는 엔드포인트는 `UseEndpoints`에서 구성됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-147">Endpoints that can be matched and executed by the app are configured in `UseEndpoints`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-148">예를 들어 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*> 및 [이들과 유사한 메서드](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions)는 요청 대리자를 라우팅 시스템에 연결합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-148">For example, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>, and [similar methods](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions) connect request delegates to the routing system.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="d8913-149">ASP.NET Core Framework 기능을 라우팅 시스템에 연결하는 데 다음과 같은 추가 메서드를 사용할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-149">Additional methods can be used to connect ASP.NET Core framework features to the routing system:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="d8913-150">[Razor Pages의 MapRazorPages](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-150">[MapRazorPages for Razor Pages](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*)</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="d8913-151">컨트롤러의 MapControllers</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-151">MapControllers for controllers</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*)
- <span data-ttu-id="d8913-152">[SignalR의 MapHub\<THub>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.HubRouteBuilder.MapHub*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-152">[MapHub\<THub> for SignalR](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.HubRouteBuilder.MapHub*)</span></span> 
- [<span data-ttu-id="d8913-153">gRPC의 MapGrpcService\<TService></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-153">MapGrpcService\<TService> for gRPC</span></span>](xref:grpc/aspnetcore)

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-154">다음 예제에서는 더 복잡한 경로 템플릿을 사용한 라우팅을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-154">The following example shows routing with a more sophisticated route template:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/RouteTemplateStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-155">`/hello/{name:alpha}` 문자열은 **경로 템플릿**이며</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-155">The string `/hello/{name:alpha}` is a **route template**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-156">엔드포인트가 일치되는 방식을 구성합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-156">It is used to configure how the endpoint is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-157">이 경우 템플릿은 다음과 일치합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-157">In this case, the template matches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-158">`/hello/Ryan`과 같은 URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-158">A URL like `/hello/Ryan`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-159">`/hello/`로 시작하고 그 다음에 시퀀스 영문자가 오는 URL 경로.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-159">Any URL path that begins with `/hello/` followed by a sequence of alphabetic characters.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="d8913-160">`:alpha`는 영문자와만 일치하는 경로 제약 조건을 적용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-160">`:alpha` applies a route constraint that matches only alphabetic characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-161">[경로 제약 조건](#route-constraint-reference)은 이 문서의 뒷부분에 설명되어 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-161">[Route constraints](#route-constraint-reference) are explained later in this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-162">URL 경로의 두 번째 세그먼트 `{name:alpha}`는 다음과 같습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-162">The second segment of the URL path, `{name:alpha}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-163">`name` 매개 변수에 바인딩됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-163">Is bound to the `name` parameter.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-164">[HttpRequest.RouteValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*)에 캡처되고 저장됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-164">Is captured and stored in [HttpRequest.RouteValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-165">이 문서에서 설명하는 엔드포인트는 라우팅 시스템은 ASP.NET Core 3.0의 새로운 기능입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-165">The endpoint routing system described in this document is new as of ASP.NET Core 3.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-166">그러나 모든 버전의 ASP.NET Core에서 동일한 경로 템플릿 기능 및 경로 제약 조건 집합을 지원합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-166">However, all versions of ASP.NET Core support the same set of route template features and route constraints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-167">다음 예제에서는 [상태 검사](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks) 및 권한 부여를 사용한 라우팅을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-167">The following example shows routing with [health checks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks) and authorization:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/AuthorizationStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

[!INCLUDE[request localized comments](~/includes/code-comments-loc.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-168">앞의 예제에서는 다음을 수행하는 방법을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-168">The preceding example demonstrates how:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-169">권한 부여 미들웨어를 라우팅에 사용할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-169">The authorization middleware can be used with routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-170">엔드포인트를 사용하여 권한 부여 동작을 구성할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-170">Endpoints can be used to configure authorization behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-171"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> 호출은 상태 검사 엔드포인트를 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-171">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> call adds a health check endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-172">이 호출에 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*>을 연결하면 권한 부여 정책이 엔드포인트에 연결됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-172">Chaining <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*> on to this call attaches an authorization policy to the endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-173"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthentication*> 및 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthorization*>을 호출하면 인증 및 권한 부여 미들웨어가 추가됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-173">Calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthentication*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthorization*> adds the authentication and authorization middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-174">이러한 미들웨어는 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*>과 `UseEndpoints` 사이에 배치되므로 다음을 수행할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-174">These middleware are placed between <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> and `UseEndpoints` so that they can:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-175">`UseRouting`에서 선택된 엔드포인트를 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-175">See which endpoint was selected by `UseRouting`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-176">엔드포인트로 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>가 디스패치되기 전에 권한 부여 정책을 적용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-176">Apply an authorization policy before <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> dispatches to the endpoint.</span></span>

<a name="metadata"></a>

### <a name="endpoint-metadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-177">엔드포인트 메타데이터</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-177">Endpoint metadata</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-178">앞의 예제에는 두 개의 엔드포인트가 있지만 상태 검사 엔드포인트에만 권한 부여 정책이 연결되어 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-178">In the preceding example, there are two endpoints, but only the health check endpoint has an authorization policy attached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-179">요청이 상태 검사 엔드포인트 `/healthz`와 일치하는 경우 권한 부여 확인이 수행됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-179">If the request matches the health check endpoint, `/healthz`, an authorization check is performed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-180">이는 엔드포인트에 추가 데이터가 연결될 수 있음을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-180">This demonstrates that endpoints can have extra data attached to them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-181">이러한 추가 데이터를 엔드포인트 **메타데이터**라고 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-181">This extra data is called endpoint **metadata**:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-182">이 메타데이터는 라우팅 인식 미들웨어에서 처리될 수 있으며</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-182">The metadata can be processed by routing-aware middleware.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-183">모든 .NET 형식일 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-183">The metadata can be of any .NET type.</span></span>

## <a name="routing-concepts"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-184">라우팅 개념</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-184">Routing concepts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-185">라우팅 시스템은 강력한 **엔드포인트** 개념을 추가하여 미들웨어 파이프라인을 기반으로 빌드됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-185">The routing system builds on top of the middleware pipeline by adding the powerful **endpoint** concept.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-186">엔드포인트는 라우팅, 권한 부여 및 ASP.NET Core 시스템 수의 측면에서 서로 다른 앱의 기능 단위를 나타냅니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-186">Endpoints represent units of the app's functionality that are distinct from each other in terms of routing, authorization, and any number of ASP.NET Core's systems.</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

### <a name="aspnet-core-endpoint-definition"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-187">ASP.NET Core 엔드포인트 정의</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-187">ASP.NET Core endpoint definition</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-188">ASP.NET Core 엔드포인트는 다음과 같습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-188">An ASP.NET Core endpoint is:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-189">실행 가능: <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>가 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-189">Executable: Has a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-190">확장 가능: [메타데이터](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*) 컬렉션이 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-190">Extensible: Has a [Metadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*) collection.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-191">Selectable: 필요에 따라 [라우팅 정보](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*)가 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-191">Selectable: Optionally, has [routing information](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-192">열거 가능: [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection)에서 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource>를 검색하여 엔드포인트 컬렉션을 나열할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-192">Enumerable: The collection of endpoints can be listed by retrieving the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-193">다음 코드에서는 현재 요청과 일치하는 엔드포인트를 검색하고 검사하는 방법을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-193">The following code shows how to retrieve and inspect the endpoint matching the current request:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/EndpointInspectorStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-194">엔드포인트는 선택된 경우 `HttpContext`에서 검색할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-194">The endpoint, if selected, can be retrieved from the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-195">해당 속성을 검사할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-195">Its properties can be inspected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-196">엔드포인트 개체는 변경할 수 없으며 만든 후 수정할 수 없습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-196">Endpoint objects are immutable and cannot be modified after creation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-197">가장 일반적인 형식의 엔드포인트는 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint>입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-197">The most common type of endpoint is a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-198">`RouteEndpoint`에는 라우팅 시스템에서 선택할 수 있는 정보가 포함됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-198">`RouteEndpoint` includes information that allows it to be to selected by the routing system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-199">앞의 코드에서 [app.Use](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.UseExtensions.Use*)는 인라인 [미들웨어](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)를 구성합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-199">In the preceding code, [app.Use](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.UseExtensions.Use*) configures an in-line [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index).</span></span>

<a name="mt"></a>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-200">다음 코드에서는 파이프라인에서 `app.Use`가 호출되는 위치에 따라 엔드포인트가 없을 수 있음을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-200">The following code shows that, depending on where `app.Use` is called in the pipeline, there may not be an endpoint:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/MiddlewareFlowStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-201">위의 샘플에서는 엔드포인트가 선택되었는지 아닌지를 표시하는 `Console.WriteLine` 문을 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-201">This preceding sample adds `Console.WriteLine` statements that display whether or not an endpoint has been selected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-202">명확하게 하도록 이 샘플에서는 제공된 `/` 엔드포인트에 표시 이름을 할당합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-202">For clarity, the sample assigns a display name to the provided `/` endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-203">`/`의 URL을 사용하여 이 코드를 실행하면 다음이 표시됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-203">Running this code with a URL of `/` displays:</span></span>

```txt
1. Endpoint: (null)
2. Endpoint: Hello
3. Endpoint: Hello
```

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-204">다른 URL을 사용하여 이 코드를 실행하면 다음이 표시됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-204">Running this code with any other URL displays:</span></span>

```txt
1. Endpoint: (null)
2. Endpoint: (null)
4. Endpoint: (null)
```

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-205">이 출력은 다음을 나타냅니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-205">This output demonstrates that:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-206">`UseRouting`을 호출하기 전에 엔드포인트는 항상 null입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-206">The endpoint is always null before `UseRouting` is called.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-207">일치 항목이 발견되면 `UseRouting`와 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>사이에서 엔드포인트가 null이 아닙니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-207">If a match is found, the endpoint is non-null between `UseRouting` and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-208">일치 항목이 발견되면 `UseEndpoints` 미들웨어가 **터미널**입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-208">The `UseEndpoints` middleware is **terminal** when a match is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-209">[터미널 미들웨어](#tm)는 이 문서의 뒷부분에 정의되어 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-209">[Terminal middleware](#tm) is defined later in this document.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-210">`UseEndpoints` 뒤의 미들웨어는 일치 항목이 없는 경우에만 실행됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-210">The middleware after `UseEndpoints` execute only when no match is found.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-211">`UseRouting` 미들웨어는 [SetEndpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) 메서드를 사용하여 엔드포인트를 현재 컨텍스트에 연결합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-211">The `UseRouting` middleware uses the [SetEndpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) method to attach the endpoint to the current context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-212">`UseRouting` 미들웨어를 사용자 지정 논리로 바꾸어도 엔드포인트를 사용하는 이점을 얻을 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-212">It's possible to replace the `UseRouting` middleware with custom logic and still get the benefits of using endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-213">엔드포인트는 미들웨어와 같은 하위 수준 기본 형식이며 라우팅 구현에 결합되지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-213">Endpoints are a low-level primitive like middleware, and aren't coupled to the routing implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-214">대부분의 앱에서는 `UseRouting`을 사용자 지정 논리로 바꿀 필요가 없습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-214">Most apps don't need to replace `UseRouting` with custom logic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-215">`UseEndpoints` 미들웨어는 `UseRouting` 미들웨어와 함께 사용하기 위한 것입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-215">The `UseEndpoints` middleware is designed to be used in tandem with the `UseRouting` middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-216">엔드포인트를 실행하는 핵심 논리는 복잡하지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-216">The core logic to execute an endpoint isn't complicated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-217"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*>를 사용하여 엔드포인트를 검색한 다음 해당 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> 속성을 호출하면 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-217">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*> to retrieve the endpoint, and then invoke its <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> property.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-218">다음 코드에서는 미들웨어가 라우팅에 영향을 주거나 반응하는 방식을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-218">The following code demonstrates how middleware can influence or react to routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/IntegratedMiddlewareStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-219">앞의 예제에서는 다음과 같은 두 가지 중요한 개념을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-219">The preceding example demonstrates two important concepts:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-220">미들웨어는 `UseRouting` 전에 실행되어 라우팅 작동의 기반이 되는 데이터를 수정할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-220">Middleware can run before `UseRouting` to modify the data that routing operates upon.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-221">일반적으로 라우팅 전에 표시되는 미들웨어는 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RewriteBuilderExtensions.UseRewriter*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HttpMethodOverrideExtensions.UseHttpMethodOverride*>또는 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.UsePathBaseExtensions.UsePathBase*>와 같은 요청의 일부 속성을 수정합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-221">Usually middleware that appears before routing modifies some property of the request, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RewriteBuilderExtensions.UseRewriter*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HttpMethodOverrideExtensions.UseHttpMethodOverride*>, or <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.UsePathBaseExtensions.UsePathBase*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-222">미들웨어는 `UseRouting`과 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> 사이에서 실행되어 엔드포인트가 실행되기 전에 라우팅의 결과를 처리할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-222">Middleware can run between `UseRouting` and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> to process the results of routing before the endpoint is executed.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-223">`UseRouting`과 `UseEndpoints` 사이에서 실행되는 미들웨어는 다음을 수행합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-223">Middleware that runs between `UseRouting` and `UseEndpoints`:</span></span>
      * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-224">일반적으로 메타데이터를 검사하여 엔드포인트를 이해합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-224">Usually inspects metadata to understand the endpoints.</span></span>
      * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-225">`UseAuthorization` 및 `UseCors`에서 하는 것처럼 보안 결정을 내리는 경우가 많습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-225">Often makes security decisions, as done by `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-226">미들웨어와 메타데이터를 조합하면 엔드포인트별로 정책을 구성할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-226">The combination of middleware and metadata allows configuring policies per-endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-227">위의 코드에서는 엔드포인트별 정책을 지원하는 사용자 지정 미들웨어의 예를 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-227">The preceding code shows an example of a custom middleware that supports per-endpoint policies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-228">이 미들웨어는 중요한 데이터에 대한 액세스의 ‘감사 로그’를 콘솔에 기록합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-228">The middleware writes an *audit log* of access to sensitive data to the console.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-229">`AuditPolicyAttribute` 메타데이터를 사용하여 엔드포인트를 ‘감사’하도록 미들웨어를 구성할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-229">The middleware can be configured to *audit* an endpoint with the `AuditPolicyAttribute` metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-230">이 샘플에서는 중요함으로 표시된 엔드포인트만 감사되는 ‘옵트인 패턴’을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-230">This sample demonstrates an *opt-in* pattern where only endpoints that are marked as sensitive are audited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-231">예를 들어 이 논리를 역으로 정의하여 안전한 것으로 표시되지 않은 모든 항목을 감사할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-231">It's possible to define this logic in reverse, auditing everything that isn't marked as safe, for example.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-232">엔드포인트 메타데이터 시스템은 유연합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-232">The endpoint metadata system is flexible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-233">이 논리는 사용 사례에 적합한 방식으로 설계할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-233">This logic could be designed in whatever way suits the use case.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-234">앞의 샘플 코드는 엔드포인트의 기본 개념을 보여 주기 위한 것입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-234">The preceding sample code is intended to demonstrate the basic concepts of endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-235">**프로덕션 용도로는 사용하지 않아야 합니다**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-235">**The sample is not intended for production use**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-236">‘감사 로그’ 미들웨어의 전체 버전은 다음과 같습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-236">A more complete version of an *audit log* middleware would:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-237">파일이나 데이터베이스에 기록합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-237">Log to a file or database.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-238">사용자, IP 주소, 중요한 엔드포인트의 이름 등과 같은 세부 정보를 포함합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-238">Include details such as the user, IP address, name of the sensitive endpoint, and more.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-239">감사 정책 메타데이터 `AuditPolicyAttribute`는 컨트롤러 및 SignalR 같은 클래스 기반 프레임워크에서 더욱 쉽게 사용할 수 있도록 `Attribute`로 정의됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-239">The audit policy metadata `AuditPolicyAttribute` is defined as an `Attribute` for easier use with class-based frameworks such as controllers and SignalR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-240">‘라우팅 대상 코드’를 사용하면 다음과 같이.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-240">When using *route to code*:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-241">메타데이터가 작성기 API와 연결됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-241">Metadata is attached with a builder API.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-242">엔드포인트를 만들 때 해당 메서드 및 클래스의 모든 특성이 클래스 기반 프레임워크에 포함됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-242">Class-based frameworks include all attributes on the corresponding method and class when creating endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-243">메타데이터 형식은 인터페이스나 특성으로 정의하는 것이 가장 좋습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-243">The best practices for metadata types are to define them either as interfaces or attributes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-244">인터페이스 및 특성을 사용하면 코드를 다시 사용할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-244">Interfaces and attributes allow code reuse.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-245">메타데이터 시스템은 유연하며 제한을 적용하지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-245">The metadata system is flexible and doesn't impose any limitations.</span></span>

<a name="tm"></a>

### <a name="comparing-a-terminal-middleware-and-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-246">터미널 미들웨어와 라우팅 비교</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-246">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-247">다음 코드 샘플에서는 미들웨어 사용과 라우팅 사용을 비교합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-247">The following code sample contrasts using middleware with using routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/TerminalMiddlewareStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-248">`Approach 1:`로 표시된 미들웨어 스타일은 **터미널 미들웨어**입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-248">The style of middleware shown with `Approach 1:` is **terminal middleware**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-249">일치 작업을 수행하기 때문에 터미널 미들웨어라고 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-249">It's called terminal middleware because it does a matching operation:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-250">위 샘플의 일치 작업은 미들웨어의 `Path == "/"`와 라우팅의 `Path == "/Movie"`입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-250">The matching operation in the preceding sample is `Path == "/"` for the middleware and `Path == "/Movie"` for routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-251">일치가 성공하면 일부 기능을 실행하고 `next` 미들웨어를 호출하는 대신 반환합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-251">When a match is successful, it executes some functionality and returns, rather than invoking the `next` middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-252">검색을 종료하고 일부 기능을 실행한 다음 반환하기 때문에 터미널 미들웨어라고 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-252">It's called terminal middleware because it terminates the search, executes some functionality, and then returns.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-253">터미널 미들웨어와 라우팅을 비교하면 다음과 같습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-253">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-254">두 방법 모두 처리 파이프라인을 종료할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-254">Both approaches allow terminating the processing pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-255">미들웨어는 `next`를 호출하는 대신 반환하여 파이프라인을 종료합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-255">Middleware terminates the pipeline by returning rather than invoking `next`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-256">엔드포인트는 항상 터미널입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-256">Endpoints are always terminal.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-257">터미널 미들웨어를 사용하면 파이프라인에서 미들웨어를 임의로 위치 지정할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-257">Terminal middleware allows positioning the middleware at an arbitrary place in the pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-258">엔드포인트는 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>의 위치에서 실행됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-258">Endpoints execute at the position of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-259">터미널 미들웨어는 임의의 코드를 사용하여 미들웨어가 일치되는 시기를 지정할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-259">Terminal middleware allows arbitrary code to determine when the middleware matches:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-260">사용자 지정 경로 일치 코드는 길어져서 올바르게 작성하기 어려울 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-260">Custom route matching code can be verbose and difficult to write correctly.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-261">라우팅은 일반적인 앱을 위한 간단한 솔루션을 제공합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-261">Routing provides straightforward solutions for typical apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-262">앱 대부분에는 사용자 지정 경로 일치 코드가 필요하지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-262">Most apps don't require custom route matching code.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-263">엔드포인트는 `UseAuthorization` 및 `UseCors` 같은 미들웨어와 상호 작용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-263">Endpoints interface with middleware such as `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-264">`UseAuthorization` 또는 `UseCors`와 함께 터미널 미들웨어를 사용하려면 권한 부여 시스템을 수동으로 조작해야 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-264">Using a terminal middleware with `UseAuthorization` or `UseCors` requires manual interfacing with the authorization system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-265">[엔드포인트](#endpoint)는 다음 두 가지를 모두 정의합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-265">An [endpoint](#endpoint) defines both:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-266">요청을 처리할 대리자</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-266">A delegate to process requests.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-267">임의 메타데이터의 컬렉션.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-267">A collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-268">메타데이터는 각 엔드포인트에 연결된 정책과 구성에 따라 횡단 관심사(Cross-Cutting Concerns)를 구현하는 데 사용됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-268">The metadata is used to implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-269">터미널 미들웨어는 효과적인 도구이지만 다음이 필요할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-269">Terminal middleware can be an effective tool, but can require:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-270">상당한 양의 코딩과 테스트</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-270">A significant amount of coding and testing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-271">원하는 수준의 유연성을 얻기 위한 다른 시스템과의 수동 통합</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-271">Manual integration with other systems to achieve the desired level of flexibility.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-272">터미널 미들웨어를 작성하기 전에 라우팅과 통합하는 것이 좋습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-272">Consider integrating with routing before writing a terminal middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-273">[또는](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*>과 통합되는 기존 터미널 미들웨어는 일반적으로 라우팅 인식 엔드포인트로 전환될 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-273">Existing terminal middleware that integrates with [Map](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) or <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*> can usually be turned into a routing aware endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-274">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16)는 다음과 같은 라우터 방식의 패턴을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-274">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16) demonstrates the pattern for router-ware:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-275"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>에 대한 확장 메서드를 작성합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-275">Write an extension method on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-276"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder.CreateApplicationBuilder*>를 사용하여 중첩된 미들웨어 파이프라인을 만듭니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-276">Create a nested middleware pipeline using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder.CreateApplicationBuilder*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-277">새 파이프라인에 미들웨어를 연결합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-277">Attach the middleware to the new pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-278">이 예제의 경우 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-278">In this case, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-279">미들웨어 파이프라인을 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>로 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*>합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-279"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*> the middleware pipeline into a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-280">`Map`을 호출하고 새 미들웨어 파이프라인을 제공합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-280">Call `Map` and provide the new middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-281">확장 메서드의 `Map`에서 제공하는 작성기 개체를 반환합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-281">Return the builder object provided by `Map` from the extension method.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-282">다음 코드에서는 [MapHealthChecks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks)를 사용하는 방법을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-282">The following code shows use of [MapHealthChecks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks):</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/AuthorizationStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-283">앞의 샘플에서는 작성기 개체를 반환하는 것이 중요한 이유를 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-283">The preceding sample shows why returning the builder object is important.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-284">작성기 개체를 반환하면 앱 개발자가 엔드포인트의 권한 부여와 같은 정책을 구성할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-284">Returning the builder object allows the app developer to configure policies such as authorization for the endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-285">이 예제에서는 상태 검사 미들웨어가 권한 부여 시스템과 직접 통합되지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-285">In this example, the health checks middleware has no direct integration with the authorization system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-286">메타데이터 시스템은 터미널 미들웨어를 사용하는 확장성 작성자에서 발생한 문제에 대응하여 만들어졌습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-286">The metadata system was created in response to the problems encountered by extensibility authors using terminal middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-287">미들웨어마다 권한 부여 시스템과의 고유한 통합을 구현하는 것은 문제가 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-287">It's problematic for each middleware to implement its own integration with the authorization system.</span></span>

<a name="urlm"></a>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-288">URL 일치</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-288">URL matching</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-289">라우팅이 들어오는 요청을 [엔드포인트](#endpoint)와 일치시키는 프로세스입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-289">Is the process by which routing matches an incoming request to an [endpoint](#endpoint).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-290">URL 경로 및 헤더의 데이터를 기반으로 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-290">Is based on data in the URL path and headers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-291">요청의 모든 데이터를 고려하도록 확장될 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-291">Can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-292">라우팅 미들웨어가 실행되면 `Endpoint`를 설정하여 현재 요청에서 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext>의 [요청 기능](xref:fundamentals/request-features)으로 값을 라우팅합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-292">When a routing middleware executes, it sets an `Endpoint` and route values to a [request feature](xref:fundamentals/request-features) on the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext> from the current request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-293">[HttpContext.GetEndpoint](<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*>)를 호출하면 엔드포인트를 가져옵니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-293">Calling [HttpContext.GetEndpoint](<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*>) gets the endpoint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-294">`HttpRequest.RouteValues`는 경로 값의 컬렉션을 가져옵니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-294">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` gets the collection of route values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-295">라우팅 미들웨어 뒤에 실행되는 [미들웨어](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)는 엔드포인트를 검사하고 작업을 수행할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-295">[Middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) running after the routing middleware can inspect the endpoint and take action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-296">예를 들어 권한 부여 미들웨어는 엔드포인트의 메타데이터 컬렉션에서 권한 부여 정책을 조사할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-296">For example, an authorization middleware can interrogate the endpoint's metadata collection for an authorization policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-297">요청 처리 파이프라인의 미들웨어가 모두 실행된 후에 선택한 엔드포인트의 대리자가 호출됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-297">After all of the middleware in the request processing pipeline is executed, the selected endpoint's delegate is invoked.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-298">엔드포인트 라우팅의 라우팅 시스템은 모든 디스패치를 결정합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-298">The routing system in endpoint routing is responsible for all dispatching decisions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-299">미들웨어는 선택된 엔드포인트에 기반으로 하여 정책을 적용하므로 다음이 중요합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-299">Because the middleware applies policies based on the selected endpoint, it's important that:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-300">디스패치나 보안 정책의 애플리케이션에 영향을 줄 수 있는 모든 결정은 라우팅 시스템 내에서 내려야 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-300">Any decision that can affect dispatching or the application of security policies is made inside the routing system.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-301">이전 버전과의 호환성을 위해 컨트롤러 또는 Razor Pages 엔드포인트 대리자가 실행되면 [RouteContext RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData)의 속성이 지금까지 수행된 요청 처리에 따라 적절한 값으로 설정됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-301">For backwards-compatibility, when a Controller or Razor Pages endpoint delegate is executed, the properties of [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) are set to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-302">`RouteContext` 형식은 이후 릴리스에서 obsolete로 표시됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-302">The `RouteContext` type will be marked obsolete in a future release:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-303">`RouteData.Values`를 `HttpRequest.RouteValues`로 마이그레이션합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-303">Migrate `RouteData.Values` to `HttpRequest.RouteValues`.</span></span>
> * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-304">`RouteData.DataTokens`를 마이그레이션하여 엔드포인트 메타데이터에서 [IDataTokensMetadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IDataTokensMetadata)를 검색합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-304">Migrate `RouteData.DataTokens` to retrieve [IDataTokensMetadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IDataTokensMetadata) from the endpoint metadata.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-305">URL 일치는 구성 가능한 일련의 단계로 작동합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-305">URL matching operates in a configurable set of phases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-306">각 단계의 출력은 일치 항목 집합입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-306">In each phase, the output is a set of matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-307">일치 항목 집합은 다음 단계에서 더욱 좁혀질 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-307">The set of matches can be narrowed down further by the next phase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-308">라우팅 구현에서는 일치하는 엔드포인트의 처리 순서를 보장하지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-308">The routing implementation does not guarantee a processing order for matching endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-309">기능한 **모든** 일치 항목이 한 번에 처리됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-309">**All** possible matches are processed at once.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-310">URL 일치 단계는 다음 순서로 수행됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-310">The URL matching phases occur in the following order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-311">ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-311">ASP.NET Core:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="d8913-312">엔드포인트와 해당 경로 템플릿 집합에 대한 URL 경로를 처리하여 일치 항목을 **모두** 수집합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-312">Processes the URL path against the set of endpoints and their route templates, collecting **all** of the matches.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="d8913-313">앞의 목록을 사용하여 경로 제약 조건이 적용되지 않는 일치 항목을 제거합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-313">Takes the preceding list and removes matches that fail with route constraints applied.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="d8913-314">앞의 목록을 사용하여 [MatcherPolicy](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy) 인스턴스 집합에서 실패하는 항목을 제거합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-314">Takes the preceding list and removes matches that fail the set of [MatcherPolicy](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy) instances.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="d8913-315">[EndpointSelector](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector)를 사용하여 앞의 목록을 통해 최종 결정을 내립니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-315">Uses the [EndpointSelector](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector) to make a final decision from the preceding list.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-316">엔드포인트 목록의 우선 순위는 다음에 따라 지정됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-316">The list of endpoints is prioritized according to:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-317">[RouteEndpoint.Order](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-317">The [RouteEndpoint.Order](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order*)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-318">[경로 템플릿 우선 순위](#rtp)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-318">The [route template precedence](#rtp)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-319"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector>에 도달할 때까지 각 단계에서 일치하는 모든 엔드포인트가 처리됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-319">All matching endpoints are processed in each phase until the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector> is reached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-320">`EndpointSelector`는 최종 단계이며,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-320">The `EndpointSelector` is the final phase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-321">일치 항목에서 가장 높은 우선 순위 엔드포인트를 가장 일치하는 항목으로 선택합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-321">It chooses the highest priority endpoint from the matches as the best match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-322">가장 일치하는 항목과 같은 우선 순위의 다른 일치 항목이 있으면 모호한 일치 예외가 throw됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-322">If there are other matches with the same priority as the best match, an ambiguous match exception is thrown.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-323">경로 우선 순위는 **더 구체적인** 경로 템플릿에 높은 우선 순위가 지정되는 기준에 따라 컴퓨팅됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-323">The route precedence is computed based on a **more specific** route template being given a higher priority.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-324">예를 들어 `/hello` 및 `/{message}` 템플릿을 가정해 보겠습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-324">For example, consider the templates `/hello` and `/{message}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-325">둘 다 URL 경로 `/hello`와 일치합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-325">Both match the URL path `/hello`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-326">`/hello`가 더 구체적이므로 우선 순위가 높습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-326">`/hello`  is more specific and therefore higher priority.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-327">일반적으로 경로 우선 순위는 실제로 사용되는 URL 체계에 가장 일치하는 항목을 선택하는 데 좋습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-327">In general, route precedence does a good job of choosing the best match for the kinds of URL schemes used in practice.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-328">모호성을 방지하는 데 필요한 경우에만 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order>를 사용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-328">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order> only when necessary to avoid an ambiguity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-329">라우팅에서 제공하는 확장성의 종류 때문에 라우팅 시스템이 모호한 경로를 미리 컴퓨팅할 수는 없습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-329">Due to the kinds of extensibility provided by routing, it isn't possible for the routing system to compute ahead of time the ambiguous routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-330">경로 템플릿 `/{message:alpha}` 및 `/{message:int}`와 같은 예제를 살펴보겠습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-330">Consider an example such as the route templates `/{message:alpha}` and `/{message:int}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-331">`alpha` 제약 조건은 영문자와만 일치합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-331">The `alpha` constraint matches only alphabetic characters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-332">`int` 제약 조건은 숫자와만 일치합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-332">The `int` constraint matches only numbers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-333">이러한 템플릿은 경로 우선 순위가 동일하지만 둘 다와 일치하는 단일 URL은 없습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-333">These templates have the same route precedence, but there's no single URL they both match.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-334">라우팅 시스템에서 시작 시 모호성 오류를 보고한 경우 이 유효한 사용 사례를 차단합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-334">If the routing system reported an ambiguity error at startup, it would block this valid use case.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
>
> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-335"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> 내의 작업 순서는 라우팅 동작에 영향을 주지 않지만 한 가지 예외가 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-335">The order of operations inside <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> doesn't influence the behavior of routing, with one exception.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-336"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> 및 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MvcAreaRouteBuilderExtensions.MapAreaRoute*>는 호출된 순서를 기준으로 해당 엔드포인트에 순서 값을 자동으로 할당합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-336"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MvcAreaRouteBuilderExtensions.MapAreaRoute*> automatically assign an order value to their endpoints based on the order they are invoked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-337">이는 이전 라우팅 구현과 동일한 보장을 제공하는 라우팅 시스템이 없이 컨트롤러의 오래된 동작을 시뮬레이트합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-337">This simulates long-time behavior of controllers without the routing system providing the same guarantees as older routing implementations.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-338">라우팅의 레거시 구현에서는 경로가 처리되는 순서에 종속된 라우팅 확장성을 구현할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-338">In the legacy implementation of routing, it's possible to implement routing extensibility that has a dependency on the order in which routes are processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-339">ASP.NET Core 3.0 이상의 엔드포인트 라우팅은 다음과 같습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-339">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 3.0 and later:</span></span>
> 
> * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-340">경로 개념이 없습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-340">Doesn't have a concept of routes.</span></span>
> * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-341">순서 지정을 보장하지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-341">Doesn't provide ordering guarantees.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-342">모든 엔드포인트가 한 번에 처리됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-342">All endpoints are processed at once.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-343">이 때문에 레거시 라우팅 시스템을 계속 사용하는 경우 [open a GitHub issue for assistance](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/issues)(지원을 위한 GitHub 문제를 시작)하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-343">If this means you're stuck using the legacy routing system, [open a GitHub issue for assistance](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/issues).</span></span>

<a name="rtp"></a>

### <a name="route-template-precedence-and-endpoint-selection-order"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-344">경로 템플릿 우선 순위 및 엔드포인트 선택 영역 순서</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-344">Route template precedence and endpoint selection order</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-345">[경로 템플릿 우선 순위](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L16)는 얼마나 구체적인지를 기준으로 각 경로 템플릿에 값을 할당하는 시스템입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-345">[Route template precedence](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L16) is a system that assigns each route template a value based on how specific it is.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-346">경로 템플릿 우선 순위의 특징은 다음과 같습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-346">Route template precedence:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-347">일반적인 사례에서 엔드포인트 순서를 조정할 필요가 없게 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-347">Avoids the need to adjust the order of endpoints in common cases.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-348">라우팅 동작에 관한 일반적인 기대에 맞추려고 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-348">Attempts to match the common-sense expectations of routing behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-349">예를 들어 `/Products/List` 및 `/Products/{id}` 템플릿을 가정해 보겠습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-349">For example, consider templates `/Products/List` and `/Products/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-350">URL 경로 `/Products/List`에 대해 `/Products/List`가 `/Products/{id}`보다 더 잘 일치한다고 합리적으로 가정할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-350">It would be reasonable to assume that `/Products/List` is a better match than `/Products/{id}` for the URL path `/Products/List`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-351">이유는 리터럴 세그먼트 `/List`가 매개 변수 세그먼트 `/{id}`보다 더 우선 순위가 높다고 간주되기 때문입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-351">The works because the literal segment `/List` is considered to have better precedence than the parameter segment `/{id}`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-352">우선 순위의 작동 방식에 대한 세부 정보는 경로 템플릿이 정의된 방법과 어느 정도 관련이 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-352">The details of how precedence works are coupled to how route templates are defined:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-353">세그먼트가 더 많은 템플릿은 더 구체적인 것으로 간주됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-353">Templates with more segments are considered more specific.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-354">리터럴 텍스트가 있는 세그먼트가 매개 변수 세그먼트보다 더 구체적인 것으로 간주됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-354">A segment with literal text is considered more specific than a parameter segment.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-355">제약 조건이 있는 매개 변수 세그먼트가 제약 조건이 없는 매개 변수 세그먼트보다 더 구체적인 것으로 간주됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-355">A parameter segment with a constraint is considered more specific than one without.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-356">복잡한 세그먼트는 제약 조건이 있는 매개 변수 세그먼트만큼 구체적인 것으로 간주됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-356">A complex segment is considered as specific as a parameter segment with a constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-357">Catch-all 매개 변수가 가장 덜 구체적입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-357">Catch-all parameters are the least specific.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-358">Catch-all 경로에 관한 중요한 내용은 [경로 템플릿 참조](#rtr)에서 **catch-all**을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-358">See **catch-all** in the [Route template reference](#rtr) for important information on catch-all routes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-359">정확한 값 참조는 [source code on GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L189)(GitHub의 소스 코드)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-359">See the [source code on GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L189) for a reference of exact values.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation-concepts"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-360">URL 생성 개념</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-360">URL generation concepts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-361">URL 생성은 다음과 같습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-361">URL generation:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-362">라우팅이 경로 값의 집합을 기반으로 하는 URL 경로를 만들 수 있는 프로세스입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-362">Is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d8913-363">엔드포인트와 이에 액세스하는 URL을 논리적으로 분리할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-363">Allows for a logical separation between endpoints and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-364">엔드포인트 라우팅에는 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API가 포함됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-364">Endpoint routing includes the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-365">`LinkGenerator`는 [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection)에서 사용할 수 있는 싱글톤 서비스입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-365">`LinkGenerator` is a singleton service available from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-366">`LinkGenerator` API는 실행 중인 요청의 컨텍스트 외부에서 사용할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-366">The `LinkGenerator` API can be used outside of the context of an executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-367">[Mvc.IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper) 및 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>를 사용하는 시나리오(예: [태그 도우미](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML 도우미 및 [작업 결과](xref:mvc/controllers/actions))는 내부적으로 `LinkGenerator` API를 사용하여 링크 생성 기능을 제공합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-367">[Mvc.IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper) and scenarios that rely on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, such as [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, and [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), use the `LinkGenerator` API internally to provide link generating capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-368">링크 생성기는 **주소** 및 **주소 체계**의 개념으로 지원됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-368">The link generator is backed by the concept of an **address** and **address schemes**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-369">주소 체계는 링크 생성을 위해 고려해야 할 엔드포인트를 결정하는 방법입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-369">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-370">예를 들어 컨트롤러 및 Razor Pages에서 많은 사용자에게 친숙한 경로 이름 및 경로 값 시나리오는 주소 체계로 구현됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-370">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from controllers and Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-371">링크 생성기는 다음 확장 메서드를 통해 컨트롤러 및 Razor Pages에 연결할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-371">The link generator can link to controllers and Razor Pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-372">이러한 메서드의 오버로드에는 `HttpContext`를 포함한 인수가 허용됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-372">Overloads of these methods accept arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-373">이러한 메서드는 기능적으로 [Url.Action](xref:System.Web.Mvc.UrlHelper.Action*) 및 [Url.Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*)와 동일하지만, 추가적인 유연성과 옵션을 제공합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-373">These methods are functionally equivalent to [Url.Action](xref:System.Web.Mvc.UrlHelper.Action*) and [Url.Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*), but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-374">`GetPath*` 메서드는 절대 경로가 포함된 URI를 생성한다는 점에서 `Url.Action` 및 `Url.Page`와 가장 비슷합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-374">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page`, in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-375">`GetUri*` 메서드는 항상 체계와 호스트를 포함한 절대 URI를 생성합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-375">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-376">`HttpContext`를 허용하는 메서드는 실행 중인 요청의 컨텍스트에서 URI를 생성합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-376">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-377">재정의되지 않는 한 실행 중인 요청의 [앰비언트](#ambient) 경로 값, URL 기본 경로, 체계 및 호스트가 사용됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-377">The [ambient](#ambient) route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-378"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>는 주소를 사용하여 호출됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-378"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-379">URI 생성은 다음 두 단계로 수행됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-379">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="d8913-380">주소는 해당 주소와 일치하는 엔드포인트 목록에 바인딩됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-380">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="d8913-381">제공된 값과 일치하는 경로 패턴을 찾을 때까지 각 엔드포인트의 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern>이 평가됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-381">Each endpoint's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern> is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-382">결과 출력은 링크 생성기에 제공된 다른 URI 부분과 결합되어 반환됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-382">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-383"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>에서 제공하는 메서드는 모든 유형의 주소에 대해 표준 링크 생성 기능을 지원합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-383">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-384">링크 생성기를 사용하는 가장 편리한 방법은 특정 주소 유형에 대한 작업을 수행하는 확장 메서드를 사용하는 것입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-384">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d8913-385">확장 메서드</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-385">Extension Method</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d8913-386">설명</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-386">Description</span></span> |
| ---------------- | ----------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="d8913-387">제공된 값에 기반한 절대 경로의 URI를 생성합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-387">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="d8913-388">제공된 값에 기반한 절대 URI를 생성합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-388">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-389"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 메서드 호출 시 다음과 같은 의미에 주의하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-389">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-390">들어오는 요청의 `GetUri*` 헤더의 유효성을 검사하지 않는 앱 구성에서는 `Host` 확장 메서드를 신중하게 사용하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-390">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-391">들어오는 요청의 `Host` 헤더의 유효성을 검사하지 않으면 신뢰할 수 없는 요청 입력이 보기 또는 페이지에 포함된 URI로 클라이언트에 다시 보내질 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-391">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view or page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-392">모든 프로덕션 앱은 알려진 유효한 값에 대해 `Host` 헤더의 유효성을 검사하도록 서버를 구성하는 것이 좋습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-392">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="d8913-393">미들웨어에서 `MapWhen` 또는 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>과 함께 `Map`를 사용할 때는 신중하게 사용하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-393">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-394">`Map*`는 실행 중인 요청의 기본 경로를 변경하여 링크 생성의 출력에 영향을 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-394">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-395">모든 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API는 기본 경로를 지정할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-395">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-396">링크 생성에 대한 `Map*`의 영향을 실행 취소하려면 빈 기본 경로를 지정합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-396">Specify an empty base path to undo the `Map*` affect on link generation.</span></span>

### <a name="middleware-example"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-397">미들웨어 예제</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-397">Middleware example</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-398">다음 예제에서는 미들웨어에서 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API를 사용하여 상점 제품을 나열하는 작업 메서드에 대한 링크를 만듭니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-398">In the following example, a middleware uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API to create a link to an action method that lists store products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-399">링크 생성기를 클래스에 주입하고 `GenerateLink`를 호출하여 앱의 모든 클래스에서 해당 링크 생성기를 사용할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-399">Using the link generator by injecting it into a class and calling `GenerateLink` is available to any class in an app:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Middleware/ProductsLinkMiddleware.cs?name=snippet)]

<a name="rtr"></a>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8913-400">경로 템플릿 참조</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-400">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d8913-401">`{}` 내의 토큰은 경로가 일치하는 경우 바인딩될 경로 매개 변수를 정의합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-401">Tokens within `{}` define route parameters that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-402">경로 세그먼트에 둘 이상의 경로 매개 변수를 정의할 수 있지만 경로 매개 변수를 리터럴 값으로 분리해야 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-402">More than one route parameter can be defined in a route segment, but route parameters  must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8913-403">예를 들어 `{controller=Home}{action=Index}`는 `{controller}` 및 `{action}` 사이에 리터럴 값이 없으므로 유효한 경로가 아닙니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-403">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="d8913-404">경로 매개 변수는 이름이 있어야 하며 지정된 추가 특성을 가질 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8913-404">Route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>
